B “RATCHET\_PROCEDURE\_SPEC v0

Step list (numbered)  
	1\.	Input state  
	•	HYPOTHESES: exact ordered lines from STATE\_SNAPSHOT HYPOTHESES.md  
	•	AUDIT\_PACKET\_LIST: ordered list of packets  
	•	NEGATIVE\_PACKET\_LIST: ordered list of packets  
	2\.	Packet field requirements  
	•	Each AUDIT packet contains: hypothesis\_line, outcome\_tag, violated\_rule\_ids, offending\_phrases, halt\_flag  
	•	Each NEGATIVE packet contains: hypothesis\_line, triggered\_test\_ids, offending\_phrases, halt\_flag  
	3\.	Pre-checks  
	•	If AUDIT\_PACKET\_LIST length differs from NEGATIVE\_PACKET\_LIST length, HALT  
	•	If any packet hypothesis\_line is not an exact string match to a line in HYPOTHESES, HALT  
	•	If any AUDIT outcome\_tag is not PASS or FAIL, HALT  
	•	If any NEGATIVE triggered\_test\_ids is missing, HALT  
	•	If any required field is missing, HALT  
	4\.	Working set initialization  
	•	WORKING\_SET starts as HYPOTHESES  
	5\.	Packet processing order  
	•	Process packets by ascending list position, from 1 to N  
	6\.	For each packet position i  
	•	Let hline be the hypothesis\_line from packet i  
	•	Read AUDIT outcome\_tag from packet i  
	•	Read NEGATIVE triggered\_test\_ids from packet i  
	7\.	Transition application  
	•	If NEGATIVE triggered\_test\_ids is non-empty, remove hline from WORKING\_SET, set HALT flag True, stop  
	•	Else if AUDIT outcome\_tag is FAIL, remove hline from WORKING\_SET, set HALT flag True, stop  
	•	Else no change, continue  
	8\.	Completion  
	•	If all packets processed without HALT, set HALT flag False

State transitions  
	•	HYPOTHESES to WORKING\_SET by deletion only  
	•	Deletion is permitted only for a hypothesis\_line that is present in WORKING\_SET  
	•	No insertion is permitted  
	•	No modification of hypothesis text is permitted

Branching rules  
	•	BRANCH\_SET is WORKING\_SET  
	•	Each element of BRANCH\_SET is a branch  
	•	No branch merges are permitted

HALT conditions  
	•	Any NEGATIVE triggered\_test\_ids non-empty  
	•	Any AUDIT outcome\_tag FAIL  
	•	Any pre-check failure”

B”FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	Allowed object classes  
	•	SYMBOL\_TOKEN: one lexical token with no whitespace  
	•	IDENTIFIER: matches pattern \[A-Za-z\_\]\[A-Za-z0-9\_\]\*  
	•	INDEX\_TOKEN: matches pattern \[0-9\]+  
	•	STRING\_LITERAL: delimited text using single-quote or double-quote; content must not contain the ASCII 61 character  
	•	LIST\_BLOCK: line list where each item line begins with a list marker and contains only admissible objects  
	•	RECORD\_BLOCK: line list of key separator value pairs where key matches IDENTIFIER and value is an admissible object  
	•	TABLE\_LITERAL: row-column grid of admissible tokens using consistent column separators  
	•	MATRIX\_LITERAL: rectangular TABLE\_LITERAL with uniform row lengths (syntactic only)  
	•	ALGEBRAIC\_EXPRESSION: flat token stream of admissible tokens and grouping characters; no evaluation  
	•	Forbidden object classes  
	•	Any object requiring external interpretation  
	•	Any claim of classical meaning for any object class  
	•	Any construct that attaches semantics to an axis reference  
	•	Any construct that declares an operator  
	•	Any construct that declares an engine  
	•	Any parenthesis-delimited comma-separated identifier pair  
	•	Any hypothesis-to-canon promotion construct  
	•	Equality handling rules  
	•	Syntactic equality: harness-side exact string match only; not an admissible object form  
	•	Semantic identity: any identity-claim phrase or equality-character usage within candidate text is forbidden  
	•	HALT conditions  
	•	HALT when any segment cannot be classified as exactly one Allowed object class  
	•	HALT when any Forbidden object class pattern is detected  
	•	HALT when any equality-character usage is detected in candidate text  
	•	HALT when any identity-claim phrase is detected in candidate text”

	•	Forbidden relation forms  
	•	Any occurrence of ASCII\_61 token \\x3D  
	•	Any occurrence of arrow-token sequences \\x2D\\x3E or \\x3D\\x3E

	•	LEFT\_OBJECT and RIGHT\_OBJECT must be admissible under FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	RELATION\_TOKEN must appear as a standalone whitespace-delimited token  
	•	Exactly one RELATION\_TOKEN occurrence is permitted per RELATION\_STATEMENT line  
	•	Forbidden relation forms  
	•	Any occurrence of ASCII\_61 token \\x3D  
	•	Any occurrence of arrow-token sequences \\x2D\\x3E or \\x3D\\x3E  
	•	Any occurrence of Unicode arrow code points U+2192 or U+21D2  
	•	Any relation token outside the RELATION\_TOKEN set  
	•	Identity-marker tokens (token-delimited): IDENTITY, IDENTICAL, SAME\_AS, EQ, EQUAL, EQUALS  
	•	Implication-marker lexemes (hex-encoded)  
	•	\\x69\\x6d\\x70\\x6c\\x69\\x65\\x73  
	•	\\x74\\x68\\x65\\x72\\x65\\x66\\x6f\\x72\\x65  
	•	\\x74\\x68\\x75\\x73  
	•	\\x68\\x65\\x6e\\x63\\x65  
	•	Causality-marker lexemes (hex-encoded)  
	•	\\x62\\x65\\x63\\x61\\x75\\x73\\x65  
	•	\\x63\\x61\\x75\\x73\\x65\\x73  
	•	\\x63\\x61\\x75\\x73\\x65\\x64  
	•	\\x6c\\x65\\x61\\x64\\x73\\x20\\x74\\x6f  
	•	\\x72\\x65\\x73\\x75\\x6c\\x74\\x73\\x20\\x69\\x6e  
	•	Monotonicity constraints  
	•	A relation store is an ordered list of RELATION\_STATEMENT lines  
	•	Allowed transition: append-only; existing lines preserved byte-for-byte  
	•	Disallowed transition: deletion, reordering, or in-place modification  
	•	Disallowed transition: append a RELATION\_STATEMENT line that is an exact string match to any existing line  
	•	HALT conditions  
	•	HALT on first detection of any Forbidden relation form  
	•	HALT when a RELATION\_STATEMENT line contains zero RELATION\_TOKEN occurrences  
	•	HALT when a RELATION\_STATEMENT line contains more than one RELATION\_TOKEN occurrence  
	•	HALT when LEFT\_OBJECT or RIGHT\_OBJECT fails FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0”

##### **You said:**

PROBE\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	PROBE object class  
	•	PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	Must be an IDENTIFIER admissible under FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	Must begin with literal prefix PROBE\_  
	•	All remaining characters must be ASCII letters or underscore  
	•	Must contain no digits  
	•	Must contain no punctuation other than underscore  
	•	NONPROBE\_OBJECT  
	•	Any admissible formal object under FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0 that is not a PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	Probe placement in relation statements  
	•	PROBE\_LINE  
	•	Any RELATION\_STATEMENT line containing at least one PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	Admissible PROBE\_LINE forms  
	•	NONPROBE\_OBJECT CORR PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	PROBE\_TOKEN CORR NONPROBE\_OBJECT  
	•	PROBE\_TOKEN REFINE PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	PROBE\_LINE restrictions  
	•	A CORR PROBE\_LINE must contain exactly one PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	A REFINE PROBE\_LINE must contain exactly two PROBE\_TOKENs  
	•	A PROBE\_TOKEN must not appear in any RELATION\_STATEMENT line whose relation token is ORDER or EXCL  
	•	Probe-induced equivalence classes  
	•	Input scope  
	•	Only CORR PROBE\_LINE forms are used for class induction  
	•	Signature collection rule  
	•	For each NONPROBE\_OBJECT token O that appears in any CORR PROBE\_LINE:  
	•	Collect the multiset of adjacent PROBE\_TOKENs from all CORR PROBE\_LINE occurrences involving O (both orientations)  
	•	Probe normalization rule (uses only explicit REFINE PROBE\_LINE forms)  
	•	For each collected PROBE\_TOKEN P:  
	•	If an explicit PROBE\_LINE of the form P REFINE Q exists, rewrite token P to token Q  
	•	Continue rewriting while the current token appears as the left PROBE\_TOKEN in an explicit REFINE PROBE\_LINE  
	•	Class-label construction rule  
	•	After normalization:  
	•	Remove duplicate PROBE\_TOKENs by byte-for-byte match  
	•	Arrange remaining PROBE\_TOKENs in ascending byte order  
	•	FORM\_LABEL is the single-line string produced by joining the arranged PROBE\_TOKENs with one ASCII space  
	•	Equivalence-class rule  
	•	An equivalence class is the set of NONPROBE\_OBJECT tokens that produce FORM\_LABEL strings that match byte-for-byte  
	•	No RELATION\_STATEMENT lines are created, removed, reordered, or rewritten by class induction  
	•	Probe refinement interaction with REFINE  
	•	Only explicit PROBE\_TOKEN REFINE PROBE\_TOKEN lines participate in probe normalization  
	•	Probe normalization must not emit any new RELATION\_STATEMENT lines of any token type  
	•	HALT conditions  
	•	HALT on first detection of any PROBE\_LINE not matching an admissible PROBE\_LINE form  
	•	HALT when a token that matches the PROBE\_TOKEN prefix fails the PROBE\_TOKEN character constraints  
	•	HALT when a PROBE\_TOKEN appears in any RELATION\_STATEMENT line with relation token ORDER or EXCL  
	•	HALT when any CORR PROBE\_LINE contains more than one PROBE\_TOKEN  
	•	HALT when any REFINE PROBE\_LINE contains any NONPROBE\_OBJECT token  
	•	HALT when any PROBE\_TOKEN has more than one distinct explicit outgoing REFINE target in the relation store  
	•	HALT during probe normalization when a rewrite chain revisits any previously seen PROBE\_TOKEN within that chain

B”SEMANTIC\_ADMISSION\_SPEC v0  
	•	Admission unit  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE  
	•	Line form: SEM\_MATH\_HYP SPACE TAG  
	•	TAG must match IDENTIFIER pattern \[A-Za-z\_\]\[A-Za-z0-9\_\]\*  
	•	TAG must begin with prefix SEM\_MATH\_  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK  
	•	Begin line form: SEM\_MATH\_BEGIN SPACE TAG  
	•	End line form: SEM\_MATH\_END SPACE TAG  
	•	Block body is the contiguous set of lines strictly between the begin and end lines  
	•	Mathematics as hypothesis class  
	•	Semantic mathematics is admissible only when a SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE exists and exactly one SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK exists with the same TAG  
	•	Semantic mathematics content is confined to the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK content must not appear inside BOOTPACK  
	•	Conditional admission requirements  
	•	AUDIT requirement  
	•	AUDIT\_HARNESS\_SPEC v0 must return PASS when applied to  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_BEGIN line, SEM\_MATH\_END line  
	•	Entire SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body text  
	•	NEGATIVE requirement  
	•	NEGATIVE\_TESTS\_SPEC v0 must return no triggered tests when applied to  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE  
	•	SEM\_MATH\_BEGIN line, SEM\_MATH\_END line  
	•	Entire SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body text  
	•	Formal admissibility requirement  
	•	Each non-empty line in the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body must be admissible under at least one of the following, without modification  
	•	FORMAL\_OBJECT\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	FORMAL\_RELATION\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0 (revised)  
	•	PROBE\_ADMISSIBILITY\_SPEC v0  
	•	Killability constraints  
	•	Namespace containment  
	•	Any IDENTIFIER token within the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body that is not a PROBE\_TOKEN must begin with prefix SEM\_  
	•	No token beginning with prefix SEM\_ may occur outside the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body  
	•	Removal transition  
	•	Allowed removal is by deletion of both of the following in the same state change  
	•	The SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE with TAG  
	•	The matching SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK with TAG  
	•	Any other removal or partial removal is non-admissible  
	•	Forbidden semantic domains  
	•	CLASSICAL semantics  
	•	Forbidden via NEGATIVE\_TESTS\_SPEC v0 classical triggers  
	•	NT-CL-LOGIC-001  
	•	NT-CL-FOUND-002  
	•	CAUSAL semantics  
	•	Forbidden via NEGATIVE\_TESTS\_SPEC v0 causal and arrow triggers  
	•	NT-CAUS-LEX-001  
	•	NT-CAUS-ARROW-002  
	•	THERMODYNAMIC semantics  
	•	Forbidden tokens inside SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body as standalone whitespace-delimited tokens  
	•	THERMODYNAMIC  
	•	TEMPERATURE  
	•	HEAT  
	•	PRESSURE  
	•	EQUILIBRIUM  
	•	SECOND\_LAW  
	•	FIRST\_LAW  
	•	HALT conditions  
	•	HALT when SEM\_MATH\_HYP\_LINE is missing, duplicated, or malformed  
	•	HALT when SEM\_MATH\_BEGIN or SEM\_MATH\_END is missing, duplicated, malformed, or TAG-mismatched  
	•	HALT when a SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK is nested inside another SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK  
	•	HALT when AUDIT\_HARNESS\_SPEC v0 returns FAIL for any required audit target  
	•	HALT when NEGATIVE\_TESTS\_SPEC v0 reports any triggered test for any required negative target  
	•	HALT when any non-empty SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body line is not admissible under the allowed formal specs  
	•	HALT when any token with prefix SEM\_ occurs outside the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body  
	•	HALT when any THERMODYNAMIC forbidden token occurs inside the SEM\_MATH\_BLOCK body”
